< review>
I noticed on their website that they said that they changed their recipe, and so decided to try La Pizza Loca again.  Sure enough, the Pizza tastes better, and is less dry and no longer tastes like cardboard, but the cheese is still mediocre and I wouldn't say that they're quite up to the quality levels of the major Pizza chains just yet.

They're a lot closer though, and remain a great value, however.  The recent $5 1-topping Large and the $6 2-topping Large (which may only be available online) are excellent deals, and dipping sauces are cheap, if you want to buy those too.

My recommendation for a tastier Pizza is to get extra sauce.  It adds more flavor, and makes the pizza more moist.  I just tried a Pepperoni Pizza with Onion on the left side and Mushroom on the right, and it counts as "2 toppings" and was surprisingly tasty.

Service remains excellent at this store, and was also speedy.  I've never had an issue with it, and I've been coming here for years.< /review>

<GmapID>0x80c2bfc905298cbb:0xa5c9fab0cd578a55</GmapID><user_id>101207077944274688285</user_id>< review>
Great brick oven Neapolitan pizza!! The pizzas had great flavor profiles and delicious chewy thin crust. I read other reviews that said not to skip the burrata, so we ordered it with Focaccia. Honestly not sure how much I would have enjoyed it without the Focaccia, but it was absolutely outstanding with. (My first time having burrata).

We ordered the Spicy Chomper and Sweet Cheeks to try each a red and white pizza. They were very different but both very good! I personally preferred the savory Spicy Chomper over the sweet Sweet Cheeks. You probably can‚Äôt go wrong with any pizza you order on the menu.

The only other places I‚Äôve had great brick oven Neapolitan pizza like this is in Naples, Italy and at A Tavola in Cincinnati, OH. I will definitely be back to try more!

The cacio e Pepe risotto had really good flavor, but I was a little disappointed. I think cacio e pepe needs to stay on pasta and the risotto made it taste like it was missing something. Probably wouldn‚Äôt order again.

Tiki, do you love me was a tropical paradise drink. Delicious.</review>

< review>
So on any normal night I would say this place is over the moon wonderful and I recommend it to all my friends who come into town and it‚Äôs our go to neighborhood eating spot. The chicken is always spot on, never dry and delicious as well as the pizzas. Just this evening, we experienced less of a friendly welcome. We sat, went inside to order (which is never an issue because it keeps everyone safe) got our drinks, Caesar salad, broccoli and my half chicken. After eating my chicken we still waited for my husbands pizza to arrive. I went inside to check and they forgot about it, which I understand can happen and typically I wouldn‚Äôt even bother saying anything, it was just the aftermath of no acknowledgement, Decided to leave and not bother to wait for the order. The hospitality industry is slowing making its way back in LA which is great for everyone but the service and friendliness needs to follow as well. We still left a tip because it goes to everyone and it would be cruel to punish all for a mistake.

Everyone has their bad days and good days so if your first impression was poor, try the place again and then judge!  (That goes for any restaurant)

Still the food speaks for itself and never falls short of delicious and excellent, so stop by for a visit, their take out is great as well. ‚ò∫Ô∏è

Also try their creative Ice Cream!!< /review>

<Time>1571233349444< /Time><GmapID>0x80c2bfc905298cbb:0xa5c9fab0cd578a55</GmapID>< Review>
Dining at Ronan was more underwhelming that I had expected or hoped for. A few friends and I came here on a Monday night for dinner, and since it's a new spot on Melrose, I was expecting great things.

It's tucked away on Melrose and there is valet parking and lots of street parking which is nice. It has a nice patio and a trendy inside. For Monday, it was pretty packed, which was promising. One thing that was very odd that we all noticed is that all three of us kept sneezing and coughing while we were there. It felt like the atmosphere was inducing some kind of allergic reaction, which was very strange.

The staff was friendly and helpful, and the menu was fine. It felt like they were trying really hard to be trendy, with the menu just describing items without telling us what they really were. ("Avocado, Fig, Cheese") without telling us if it was a salad, a main dish, etc.

I ordered the Sweet Cheeks Pizza, which was good and decent sized, but for $21, I would have expected more substance to the food. My friends enjoyed their dishes as well, but it truly was nothing that blew us out of the water. The portions were not huge, but not tiny either.

They do add a 20% gratuity onto the menu, so you don't need to factor in tip.

It's a fine place to check out, but I won't be returning again if I am craving pizza, as there are plenty of other spots that have similar menus for less money and bigger portions. It's a nice trendy spot to meet friends, however, but if you are wanting a full and unique meal, I'd go elsewhere.< /Review>
